    4512             : //  void Unparser::printDeclModifier
    4513             : //  void Unparser::printAccessModifier   
    4514             : //  void Unparser::printStorageModifier
    4515             : //  
    4516             : //  The following 2 functions: printAccessModifier and printStorageModifier,
    4517             : //  are just the two halves from printDeclModifier. These two functions
    4518             : //  are used in the unparse functions for SgMemberFunctionDeclarations
    4519             : //  and SgVariableDeclaration.  printAccessModifier is first called before
    4520             : //  the format function. If "private", "protected", or "public" is to
    4521             : //  be printed out, it does so here. Then I format which will put me
    4522             : //  in position to unparse the declaration. Then I call
    4523             : //  printSpecifer2, which will print out any keywords if the option is
    4524             : //  turned on.  Then the declaration is printed in the same line. If I
    4525             : //  didnt do this, the printing of keywords would be done before
    4526             : //  formatting, and would put the declaration on another line (and
    4527             : //  would look terribly formatted).
